grew up in a small town in Northern Wiscosin so I am defeintately a Cheesehead and Badgers fan.  I played numerous sports growing up but my favorite ones were basketball, wrestling, and golf.   I attended the University of Wisconsin Superior where I majored in Physical Education and minored in Coaching.  I graduated in 2005 and have been in Lake County ever since. Physical Education is my life and I want to share my passion by making my classes challenging, engaging, and ecudational.  I have been teaching the drivers education course Behind the Wheel since 2008 so I get to see former PE students now at the high school level.  From 20012-present,  I have been the Grade Level Chair for Special Area Teachers.   If you have any questions or concerns please feel free to contact me at
